If you have 3 apples and take away 2, how many do YOU have?
Starting with 3 apples.
Take away 2.
3 - 2 = 1 apple remains.
Wait,
The question asks how many YOU have.
YOU took 2 apples.
So YOU have 2.
Answer: 2

---

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.
Answer: 1
Answer: 1

Calculate: ((14 * 4) + 9) / 4
First, 14 * 4 = 56
Then, 56 + 9 = 65
Finally, 65 / 4 = 16
Answer: 16

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
The farmer lost some sheep.
17 sheep total, some ran away.
If all but 9 ran away, then 17 - 9 = 8 ran away.
So 17 - 8 = 9 are left... wait, that's circular.
Actually,
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.
Answer: 9

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
25 / 5 = 5.
So you can subtract 5 times.
Wait, let me verify: 25-5=20, 20-5=15, 15-5=10, 10-5=5, 5-5=0.
Yes, 5 times.
Hold on,
You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.
Answer: 1
Answer: 1

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
25 / 5 = 5.
So you can subtract 5 times.
Wait, let me verify: 25-5=20, 20-5=15, 15-5=10, 10-5=5, 5-5=0.
Yes, 5 times.
Hold on,
You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.
Answer: 1
Answer: 1

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
The farmer lost some sheep.
17 sheep total, some ran away.
If all but 9 ran away, then 17 - 9 = 8 ran away.
So 17 - 8 = 9 are left... wait, that's circular.
Wait,
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.
Answer: 9

Calculate: ((8 * 2) + 4) / 5
First, 8 * 2 = 16
Then, 16 + 4 = 20
Finally, 20 / 5 = 4
Answer: 4

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
The farmer lost some sheep.
17 sheep total, some ran away.
If all but 9 ran away, then 17 - 9 = 8 ran away.
So 17 - 8 = 9 are left... wait, that's circular.
Let me reconsider,
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.
Answer: 9

---

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
The farmer lost some sheep.
17 sheep total, some ran away.
If all but 9 ran away, then 17 - 9 = 8 ran away.
So 17 - 8 = 9 are left... wait, that's circular.
Let me reconsider,
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.
Answer: 9

---

Calculate: ((30 * 9) + 3) / 4
First, 30 * 9 = 270
Then, 270 + 3 = 273
Finally, 273 / 4 = 68
Answer: 68

---

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.
Answer: 1
Answer: 1

If you have 3 apples and take away 2, how many do YOU have?
Starting with 3 apples.
Take away 2.
3 - 2 = 1 apple remains.
Hold on,
The question asks how many YOU have.
YOU took 2 apples.
So YOU have 2.
Answer: 2

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
25 / 5 = 5.
So you can subtract 5 times.
Wait, let me verify: 25-5=20, 20-5=15, 15-5=10, 10-5=5, 5-5=0.
Yes, 5 times.
Let me reconsider,
You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.
Answer: 1
Answer: 1

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
The farmer lost some sheep.
17 sheep total, some ran away.
If all but 9 ran away, then 17 - 9 = 8 ran away.
So 17 - 8 = 9 are left... wait, that's circular.
Let me reconsider,
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.
Answer: 9

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
25 / 5 = 5.
So you can subtract 5 times.
Wait, let me verify: 25-5=20, 20-5=15, 15-5=10, 10-5=5, 5-5=0.
Yes, 5 times.
Hold on,
You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.
Answer: 1
Answer: 1

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
25 / 5 = 5.
So you can subtract 5 times.
Wait, let me verify: 25-5=20, 20-5=15, 15-5=10, 10-5=5, 5-5=0.
Yes, 5 times.
Hold on,
You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.
Answer: 1
Answer: 1

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
The farmer lost some sheep.
17 sheep total, some ran away.
If all but 9 ran away, then 17 - 9 = 8 ran away.
So 17 - 8 = 9 are left... wait, that's circular.
Actually,
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.
Answer: 9

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
The farmer lost some sheep.
17 sheep total, some ran away.
If all but 9 ran away, then 17 - 9 = 8 ran away.
So 17 - 8 = 9 are left... wait, that's circular.
Actually,
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.
Answer: 9

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
The farmer lost some sheep.
17 sheep total, some ran away.
If all but 9 ran away, then 17 - 9 = 8 ran away.
So 17 - 8 = 9 are left... wait, that's circular.
Hold on,
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.

This seems like a weight estimation problem.
Average weight for 5'10" is around 160-180 lbs.
Estimate: 170 lbs.
Let me reconsider,
A butcher shop clerk weighs MEAT.
That's his job - to weigh meat for customers.
The answer is: meat (or 0 for numerical).
Answer: 0

Next number might be 15.
I should have

Pattern: 5, 2, 7, 9
Next: 16
Answer: 16

YOU took 2 apples.
So YOU have 2.

---

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
The farmer lost some sheep.
17 sheep total, some ran away.
If all but 9 ran away, then 17 - 9 = 8 ran away.
So 17 - 8 = 9 are left... wait, that's circular.
Hold on,
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.
Answer: 9

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
25 / 5 = 5.
So you can subtract 5 times.
Wait, let me verify: 25-5=20, 20-5=15, 15-5=10, 10-5=5, 5-5=0.
Yes, 5 times.
Actually,
You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.
Answer: 1
Answer: 1

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
25 / 5 = 5.
So you can subtract 5 times.
Wait, let me verify: 25-5=20, 20-5=15, 15-5=10, 10-5=5, 5-5=0.

You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.

Answer: 1

---

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
25 / 5 = 5.
So you can subtract 5 times.
Wait, let me verify: 25-5=20, 20-5=15, 15-5=10, 10-5=5, 5-5=0.
Yes, 5 times.
Hold on,
You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.
Answer: 1
Answer: 1

---

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
The farmer lost some sheep.
17 sheep total, some ran away.
If all but 9 ran away, then 17 - 9 = 8 ran away.
So 17 - 8 = 9 are left... wait, that's circular.
Hold on,
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.
Answer: 9

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.
Answer: 1
Answer: 1

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
25 / 5 = 5.
So you can subtract 5 times.
Wait, let me verify: 25-5=20, 20-5=15, 15-5=10, 10-5=5, 5-5=0.
Yes, 5 times.
Actually,
You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.
Answer: 1
Answer: 1

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
The farmer lost some sheep.
17 sheep total, some ran away.
If all but 9 ran away, then 17 - 9 = 8 ran away.
So 17 - 8 = 9 are left... wait, that's circular.
Let me reconsider,
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.
Answer: 9

A butcher shop clerk weighs MEAT.

---

How many times can you subtract 5 from 25?
25 / 5 = 5.
So you can subtract 5 times.
Wait, let me verify: 25-5=20, 20-5=15, 15-5=10, 10-5=5, 5-5=0.
Yes, 5 times.
Actually,
You can only subtract 5 from 25 ONCE.
After that, you're subtracting from 20, not 25.
Answer: 1
Answer: 1

---

Next: 16
Answer: 16

Calculate: ((16 * 8) + 4) / 4
First, 16 * 8 = 128
Then, 128 + 4 = 132
Finally, 132 / 4 = 33
Answer: 33

If you have 3 apples and take away 2, how many do YOU have?
The question asks how many YOU have.
YOU took 2 apples.
So YOU have 2.
Answer: 2

---

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.
Answer: 9

---

A farmer has 17 sheep. All but 9 run away. How many are left?
The farmer lost some sheep.
17 sheep total, some ran away.
If all but 9 ran away, then 17 - 9 = 8 ran away.
So 17 - 8 = 9 are left... wait, that's circular.
Actually,
"All but 9" means 9 remain.
So the answer is simply 9.
Answer: 9
